< review>
Saw this place on Diners Dives and Drive Ins (never actually seen a drive in on the show). Anyhow, was very eager to bring the family there to show off the incredible selection of dogs, kielbasa, chicken breast, etc.,

In line about to order for everyone, wife needed to use the restroom.  The cashier lady refused to give my wife the key to the bathroom. She rudely replied saying only after we pay for the food. Okay, we respect company policy that bathrooms are reserved for customers, but we were ordering when she made that comment. My wife was not very happy and I agreed with her. This place did not deserve our business. The disrespect from her was unbelievable.  Not to mention, in the short time there, the place was beginning to feel like a hangout for junkies. Became a very uncomfortable place to be, so we left and gave the bad attitude cashier a piece of our mind.

Sad, was hoping this would have been a positive and memorable lunchtime experience. Far from it. Watch your back, undesirable crowds seem to dwell there.</review>

< Review>
This being Mid-Market district, expect to pay a premium for your fare and believe me it's worth every bite. Once I save my money up again, this will be my first stop for lunch.
While the district is going through some much needed upgrades.
Show Dogs, has planted itself as a mainstay for now. The atmosphere comes to light when you take a seat and catch the outside foot traffic. The City's homeless at their best. Open air drug dealing could also catch your amazement while dinning. But the food will bring you back over and over again. Yeah, the food is that good.<//Review>

< Text>
This is Kimball recreation center and park. There's a walking, jogging, running trial that runs the perimeter of the park...bikes can use it too. There's lots of open grass fields for playing and running your dog, and soccer fields. There's a beautiful aquatic center with a fun Children's area, two giant water slides, an Olympic sized pool, and a lap pool. I think every Thursday there's a farmer's market that sets up in the parking lot. There's also a couple electric car charging hookups.<//Text>

<rating>5<//rating><text>I walked in and was gifted with the faintest smell of pizza in the oven and subs on the grill. Immediately, I was welcomed by both nostalgia, and a sense of wonder and optimism I had not been acquainted with in years. I walked through the store, taking in the wall decorations and lights and weirdly felt at home in a place I had never been too. I ordered my usual, small cheese pizza with grilled chicken, as well as a root beer. I was so surprised by how nice and devoted the staff looked. Each member looked dedicated to not only their craft, but to giving each and every guest the best possible experience. My order came out after what felt like just a couple of minutes, and I took it with a bit of excitement I hadn't ever felt before at a routine pizza joint. But nothing I felt compared to the emotions of my first slice. As I took the bite, I was transported to a world of my own. The burst of flavor not only was delicious, but it took me to a state of bliss, and made me forget all my troubles and errands. I am not a religious person, but this is the closest I have felt to ever having faith. The meal was a short one, but it was an amazing one. I left Ricky's feeling like a new person, with new goals, new emotions, and most importantly a new outlook on life. I called many members of my family whom I had not talked too in several months, and I had one of my best sleeps in recent memory. I always like to say thank you to a staff member when I leave a restaurant, but this was the first time in a very long time that I truly, and sincerely, meant it.<//text><pics>None</pics><resp>None</resp><gmapID>0x80ec139a2318c3a5:0xaac32f7f31af839e<//gmapID></record>

I have received a pedicure from here and quite enjoyed it. Tools were clean, I was offered a beverage(mimosa was an option), they were efficient and my toes looked good.  I decided to get a gel manicure on a Friday evening. I wanted the cool hombre style, but they lady said she couldn't do it. No biggie, but a bit of a bummer.  She was nice and did a pretty good, I was happy with my nails. Here's where the loss of stars comes in, my nails began to chip the next morning! One little chip, I'll get over it, not happy, but I'll get over it. Day two, I had THREE nails chipped with some good chunks missing from two, so I decided I was going to go back and have them fix my nails on Monday because that was my next available day. So prepared to request a fix, a fourth nail chips, and I decided forget it. I was able to peel all of my gel polish off in about 5 minutes without any tools or acetone.

Bottom line: GET a pedicure here, DON'T get a gel manicure< /review>

<rate>4< /rate><Text>We wanted breakfast burritos and found this place on Uber Eats. The food was delivered in less than 15 minutes! The burritos were also half the price of any other breakfast burritos I could find in the area. Pasadena is way too bougie for me sometimes, but Bobby's keeps it real.

We ordered 2 of the bacon breakfast burritos, and threw in some zucchini fries and jalapeno fries for good measure. Why not? The burritos were dense and HEAVY. I usually eat half of one and save the rest, but I couldn't get through half. I loved the thick, greasy tortilla they used and it was loaded with bacon, eggs and cheese, with less potato filler. The zucchini and jalapenos came in a box of each with ranch dressing, and were great, too.

If you had too much fun the night before, or just want a good, quality breakfast burrito, this one is solid!</Text><Resp>None<//Resp><Pictures>None< /Pictures><user_name>Bridget Penn<//user_name><Date>1559839040615</Date></record></dataset><record>

< Review>
Love this place! The spuderito with beef is amazing; I have been eaten their taco bowl for lunch two days in a row. It is so, so good. It is served in a giant fried tortilla, a layer of beans, iceberg lettuce, ground beef and tomato tossed in a green cilantro dressing. It's then topped off with some shredded cheese and I buy a container of ranch on the side. The owner Bobby and everyone there are super friendly as well. Give it a try!< /Review>

< review>
Upon arriving in the area, the parking is across the street but limited in spaces. If needed, there is some street/neighborhood parking. Staff was accommodating for my large party of seven + one dog. We didn't wait too long for a table luckily and we're immediately seated away from other tables per Covid-19 precautions. Our server Hector was very funny and gave great suggestions of what to order. He served us to the best of his abilities and was wearing a mask as well as gloves to make sure we were comfortable dining here. I was not disappointed with each dish ordered from what Hector suggested. The eggs benevilla, the eggs Nouveau, the peanut butter bacon banana bacon french toast sandwich and the beignets were delicious. I hope to be back when I'm in the area again.<//review>

Cafe Nouveau has always offered patio dinning. We miss this place post Covid and decided to try the new way of Covid dinning! CN has put in very thoughtful measures - masks, gloves for the wait staff; the process of only certain staff will clear the used plates and flatware; the way to pay bills. They separated the tables, added aluminum shields to the screens that separated the tables. We were dining in private !! We felt safety measures were satisfactory to us.<//text>

We shared an order of bacon maple beignets
They were absolutely decadent! Lots of bacon crumbles, a good amount of maple syrup

I ordered the bacon, gorgonzola & caramelized onion frittata
It comes topped with diced tomatoes and arugula

The bacon flavor was more subtle than I'd prefer, the tomatoes and arugula added a nice, refreshing layer to the profile

My youngest daughter had chocolate brioche French toast
Pure decadence: a mountain of bananas, strawberries, and whipped cream, atop two slices of midnight dark French toast, a generous helping of nutella between them

Amazing flavor

My oldest daughter had the peanut butter, bacon, banana French toast sandwich
Two slices of Texas toast sized bread surrounded a dazzling mixture of PB, bacon, and bananas, and is served with a thick maple sauce

Incredible flavor

My dish came with a cornbread blueberry muffin
Different, but tasty, warmed, with butter

The check came with three miniature lemon poppy seed muffins with frosting and sprinkles
A delicious end to a great meal</review>

<Review>Besides the exceptional food and amazing service, Café Nouveau takes the Covid-19 restrictions very seriously and installed an array of measures (great to see!):
- apart from the mandatory mask, your temperature gets checked before entering
- all menus are virtual (no sharing with previous guests)
- coffee refills are done by serving a new mug (no sharing of refill coffee pots with other guests)

<text>This restaurant is literally built in a house. It's super charming and they definitely embrace the New Orleans vibe.
Our group had a variety of things; The s'mores pancakes - SUPER sweet so I'd recommend splitting then unless you want to experience a huge sugar crash. The Poblano Del Mar - delicious but it's a lot for one person to take down - The rice was well seasoned, the pepper was well-cooked and wasn't mushy and the seafood and veggies meshed well with the entire dish. The one dish that was a little lackluster were the chocolate waffles - instead of having the chocolate chips mixed into the batter, they were out on top and therefore ended up burnt. So the waffle was really a plain waffle with burnt chocolate pieces, which was... Not great and went unfinished.

Overall though, yummy food, great service and a pretty short wait considering how busy it is.<//text><pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipO0Rs9w2nubXuIf58BpWUotplfYVOPxufdQkTiA=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipME9nlju1v1nzLXzutS1LdtZrK3BKEAgQrJ9xfA=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /pics>< response>

Don’t drive right by! Nestled in its lush garden setting in a quiet Ventura neighborhood, you might miss Cafe Nouveaux. But seek it out. It’s unique setting in an artfully re-purposed home is just the beginning of your enjoyment. Then comes the friendly and efficient staff and the great menu offering unique and delicious creations. < Text>
If I could think of my favorite reason to come to Ventura this should be the first place I’d go to and this would always be my answer.

Don’t be surprised if you have to wait 10 or 15 minutes after 9 o’clock because the whole town likes to come here… And why wouldn’t they? It’s fantastic!

I have to tell you the peanut butter and chocolate cake needs to be kept a secret because if I saw that and ordered it when I first arrived it would be all I eat LOL!

I went for the breakfast sandwich which is perfect the bun that serve done is nice and tender but does it get all sloppy and gross after a few minutes… It stayed delicious the whole time… And didn’t get a single stain on my white T-shirt.

If you like healthy salads look no further although I didn’t order the chicken salad the person I was with did it was almost so beautiful I hated seeing it be consumed LOL!

But let’s just say this the service is great I had so much fun it was like visiting a bunch of friends I hope I get to come back and see them all again!!< /Text>
